@soviet_collapse_focus_short = 4
@soviet_collapse_focus_medium = 6
@soviet_collapse_focus_long = 8

# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 CUSTOM SPLINTER FOCUS TREES
# ============================================================================
# Runtime focus packages for custom high-chaos Soviet Collapse successors.
# These tags are created during failed containment routes and use shared
# dynamic support effects plus tag-specific endgame hooks. The layout uses
# wide branch lanes with compressed depth so crisis choices do not stack into
# narrow vertical columns, while continuous focus panels sit to the right.
# ============================================================================

focus_tree = {
	id = FTH_soviet_collapse_focus_tree

	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 20
			tag = FTH
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
		}
	}
